    63	
    64	
    65	def family_results(objects: dict[str, object], metric: np.ndarray) -> dict[int, dict[str, object]]:
    66	    scalar = {key: objects[key] for key in ("R", "H", "D")}
    67	    return {
    68	        mask: reconstructed.independent.classify(
    69	            reconstructed.independent.operators(objects, keys),
    70	            objects["gradient"], metric, scalar, keys,
    71	        )
    72	        for _family_id, mask, keys in reconstructed.FAMILIES
    73	    }
    74	
    75	
    76	def labels(result: dict[str, object]) -> list[tuple[int, str]]:
    77	    return [(int(item["rank"]), str(item["signature"])) for item in result["blocks"]]
    78	
    79	
    80	def assignment(
    81	    first: dict[str, object],
    82	    second: dict[str, object],
    83	    first_projectors: list[np.ndarray] | None = None,
    84	    second_projectors: list[np.ndarray] | None = None,
    85	) -> tuple[int, ...] | None:
    86	    first_labels = labels(first)
    87	    second_labels = labels(second)
    88	    if Counter(first_labels) != Counter(second_labels):
    89	        return None
    90	    left = first_projectors or [np.asarray(item) for item in first["projectors"]]
    91	    right = second_projectors or [np.asarray(item) for item in second["projectors"]]
    92	    best: tuple[int, ...] | None = None
    93	    best_distance = math.inf
    94	    for permutation in itertools.permutations(range(len(right))):
    95	        if any(first_labels[index] != second_labels[permutation[index]] for index in range(len(left))):
    96	            continue
    97	        distance = max(
    98	            (reconstructed.independent.relmax(left[index], right[permutation[index]])
    99	             for index in range(len(left))),
   100	            default=0.0,
   101	        )
   102	        if distance < best_distance:
   103	            best = tuple(permutation)
   104	            best_distance = distance
   105	    return best
   106	
   107	
   108	def polynomial_map_value(
   109	    jacobian: np.ndarray,
   110	    jacobian_first: np.ndarray,
   111	    jacobian_second: np.ndarray,
   112	    point: np.ndarray,
   113	) -> np.ndarray:
   114	    return (
   115	        jacobian @ point
   116	        + 0.5 * np.einsum("mab,a,b->m", jacobian_first, point, point)
   117	        + (1.0 / 6.0) * np.einsum("mabc,a,b,c->m", jacobian_second, point, point, point)
   118	    )
   119	
   120	
   121	def polynomial_map_local_jets(
   122	    jacobian: np.ndarray,
   123	    jacobian_first: np.ndarray,
   124	    jacobian_second: np.ndarray,
   125	    point: np.ndarray,
   126	) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
   127	    local_jacobian = (
   128	        jacobian
   129	        + np.einsum("mab,b->ma", jacobian_first, point)
   130	        + 0.5 * np.einsum("mabc,b,c->ma", jacobian_second, point, point)
   131	    )
   132	    local_first = jacobian_first + np.einsum("mabc,c->mab", jacobian_second, point)
   133	    return local_jacobian, local_first, jacobian_second
   134	
   135	
   136	def invert_polynomial_map(
   137	    jacobian: np.ndarray,
   138	    jacobian_first: np.ndarray,
   139	    jacobian_second: np.ndarray,
   140	    target: np.ndarray,
   141	) -> tuple[np.ndarray, float]:
   142	    point = np.linalg.solve(jacobian, target)
   143	    for _iteration in range(30):
   144	        local_jacobian, _local_first, _local_second = polynomial_map_local_jets(
   145	            jacobian, jacobian_first, jacobian_second, point
   146	        )
   147	        residual = polynomial_map_value(
   148	            jacobian, jacobian_first, jacobian_second, point
   149	        ) - target
   150	        step = np.linalg.solve(local_jacobian, residual)
   151	        point -= step
   152	        if float(np.max(np.abs(step))) < 1.0e-14:
   153	            break
   154	    residual = float(np.max(np.abs(
   155	        polynomial_map_value(jacobian, jacobian_first, jacobian_second, point) - target
   156	    )))
   157	    if residual > 1.0e-11:
   158	        raise AssertionError(f"polynomial map inversion {residual}")
   159	    return point, residual
   160	
   161	
   162	def covariance_audit() -> dict[str, object]:
   163	    lookup = reconstructed.identity_data()
   164	    identities = sorted(
   165	        lookup,
   166	        key=lambda value: hashlib.sha256(
   167	            ("MOTIF_HOPF_INDEPENDENT_V1|" + value).encode()
   168	        ).hexdigest(),
   169	    )[:64]
   170	    transforms = reconstructed.independent.transforms()
   171	    comparisons = 0
   172	    nonuncertain_discordances = 0
   173	    maximum_object_residual = 0.0
   174	    maximum_projector_residual = 0.0
   175	    maximum_inverse_map_residual = 0.0
   176	    minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant = math.inf
   177	    point_status_census: Counter[str] = Counter()
   178	    edge_comparisons = 0
   179	    edge_discordances = 0
   180	    edge_total = 0
   181	    edge_skips: Counter[str] = Counter()
   182	
   183	    for identity_id in identities:
   184	        bank, amplitudes = lookup[identity_id]
   185	        original_nodes: list[dict[int, dict[str, object]]] = []
   186	        transformed_nodes: dict[str, list[dict[int, dict[str, object]]]] = {
   187	            transform_id: [] for transform_id, *_rest in transforms
   188	        }
   189	        point_maps: dict[str, list[dict[int, tuple[int, ...] | None]]] = {
   190	            transform_id: [] for transform_id, *_rest in transforms
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        for point in reconstructed.path_points(bank):
   194	            g, dg, ddg, phi_first, phi_second = reconstructed.metric_phi_jets(
   195	                bank, amplitudes, point
   196	            )
   197	            objects, _geometry = reconstructed.independent.objects(
   198	                g, dg, ddg, phi_first, phi_second
   199	            )
   200	            originals = family_results(objects, g)
   201	            original_nodes.append(originals)
   202	
   203	            for transform_id, registered_jacobian, registered_first, registered_second in transforms:
   204	                mapped_point, inverse_residual = invert_polynomial_map(
   205	                    registered_jacobian, registered_first, registered_second, point
   206	                )
   207	                jacobian, jacobian_first, jacobian_second = polynomial_map_local_jets(
   208	                    registered_jacobian, registered_first, registered_second, mapped_point
   209	                )
   210	                determinant = abs(float(np.linalg.det(jacobian)))
   211	                minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant = min(
   212	                    minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant, determinant
   213	                )
   214	                maximum_inverse_map_residual = max(
   215	                    maximum_inverse_map_residual, inverse_residual
   216	                )
   217	                transformed = reconstructed.independent.transform_jets(
   218	                    g, dg, ddg, 0.0, phi_first, phi_second,
   219	                    jacobian, jacobian_first, jacobian_second,
   220	                )
   221	                transformed_objects, _transformed_geometry = reconstructed.independent.objects(
   222	                    transformed[0], transformed[1], transformed[2],
   223	                    transformed[4], transformed[5],
   224	                )
   225	                transformed_results = family_results(transformed_objects, transformed[0])
   226	                transformed_nodes[transform_id].append(transformed_results)
   227	                inverse = np.linalg.inv(jacobian)
   228	                maximum_object_residual = max(
   229	                    maximum_object_residual,
   230	                    reconstructed.independent.relmax(transformed_objects["metric"], jacobian.T @ g @ jacobian),
   231	                    reconstructed.independent.relmax(transformed_objects["gradient"], inverse @ objects["gradient"]),
   232	                    reconstructed.independent.relmax(transformed_objects["R"], inverse @ objects["R"] @ jacobian),
   233	                    reconstructed.independent.relmax(transformed_objects["H"], inverse @ objects["H"] @ jacobian),
   234	                    reconstructed.independent.relmax(transformed_objects["D"], inverse @ objects["D"] @ jacobian),
   235	                )
   236	                current_maps: dict[int, tuple[int, ...] | None] = {}
   237	                for _family_id, mask, _keys in reconstructed.FAMILIES:
   238	                    original = originals[mask]
   239	                    current = transformed_results[mask]
   240	                    comparisons += 1
   241	                    discordant = [field for field in COMPARE if original[field] != current[field]]
   242	                    both_classified = (
   243	                        original["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED"
   244	                        and current["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED"
   245	                    )
   246	                    if both_classified:
   247	                        point_status_census["BOTH_CLASSIFIED"] += 1
   248	                    elif (
   249	                        original["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED"
   250	                    ) != (
   251	                        current["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED"
   252	                    ):
   253	                        point_status_census["ONE_SIDED_UNCERTAIN"] += 1
   254	                    else:
   255	                        point_status_census["BOTH_UNCERTAIN"] += 1
   256	                    if both_classified and discordant:
   257	                        nonuncertain_discordances += 1
   258	                    predicted = [inverse @ np.asarray(item) @ jacobian for item in original["projectors"]]
   259	                    if both_classified and not discordant:
   260	                        residual = reconstructed.independent.set_distance(
   261	                            predicted,
   262	                            [np.asarray(item) for item in current["projectors"]],
   263	                        )
   264	                        maximum_projector_residual = max(maximum_projector_residual, residual)
   265	                    current_maps[mask] = assignment(original, current, predicted)
   266	                point_maps[transform_id].append(current_maps)
   267	
   268	        # Compare the actual minimum-distance edge assignment with the assignment predicted by
   269	        # pointwise tensor covariance. This is the preregistered path-matching covariance gate.
   270	        for transform_id, *_rest in transforms:
   271	            current_nodes = transformed_nodes[transform_id]
   272	            maps = point_maps[transform_id]
   273	            for node in range(16):
   274	                for _family_id, mask, _keys in reconstructed.FAMILIES:
   275	                    left = original_nodes[node][mask]
   276	                    right = original_nodes[node + 1][mask]
   277	                    transformed_left = current_nodes[node][mask]
   278	                    transformed_right = current_nodes[node + 1][mask]
   279	                    original_edge = assignment(left, right)
   280	                    transformed_edge = assignment(transformed_left, transformed_right)
   281	                    left_map = maps[node][mask]
   282	                    right_map = maps[node + 1][mask]
   283	                    edge_total += 1
   284	                    if None in (original_edge, transformed_edge, left_map, right_map):
   285	                        reasons = []
   286	                        if original_edge is None:
   287	                            reasons.append("ORIGINAL_EDGE_UNMATCHED")
   288	                        if transformed_edge is None:
   289	                            reasons.append("TRANSFORMED_EDGE_UNMATCHED")
   290	                        if left_map is None:
   291	                            reasons.append("LEFT_POINT_COVARIANCE_MAP_UNMATCHED")
   292	                        if right_map is None:
   293	                            reasons.append("RIGHT_POINT_COVARIANCE_MAP_UNMATCHED")
   294	                        edge_skips["+".join(reasons)] += 1
   295	                        continue
   296	                    predicted = [None] * len(left_map)
   297	                    for original_left, transformed_left_index in enumerate(left_map):
   298	                        original_right = original_edge[original_left]
   299	                        predicted[transformed_left_index] = right_map[original_right]
   300	                    edge_comparisons += 1
   301	                    if tuple(predicted) != transformed_edge:
   302	                        edge_discordances += 1
   303	
   304	    return {
   305	        "coordinate_map_interpretation": MAP_INTERPRETATION,
   306	        "coordinate_map_evidence_status": "CONFIRMATORY_POST_SECOND_REVIEW_REPAIR",
   307	        "blind_identities": len(identities),
   308	        "stored_nonlinear_transforms": len(transforms),
   309	        "all_family_node_comparisons": comparisons,
   310	        "nonuncertain_classification_discordances": nonuncertain_discordances,
   311	        "maximum_intrinsic_object_covariance_residual": maximum_object_residual,
   312	        "maximum_projector_set_covariance_residual": maximum_projector_residual,
   313	        "maximum_inverse_map_residual": maximum_inverse_map_residual,
   314	        "minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant": minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant,
   315	        "point_status_census": dict(sorted(point_status_census.items())),
   316	        "uncertainty_bearing_point_comparisons": (
   317	            point_status_census["ONE_SIDED_UNCERTAIN"]
   318	            + point_status_census["BOTH_UNCERTAIN"]
   319	        ),
   320	        "possible_edge_transport_comparisons": edge_total,
   321	        "matched_edge_transport_comparisons": edge_comparisons,
   322	        "skipped_edge_transport_comparisons": sum(edge_skips.values()),
   323	        "skipped_edge_reason_census": dict(sorted(edge_skips.items())),
   324	        "matched_edge_transport_discordances": edge_discordances,
   325	    }
   326	
   327	
   328	def symbolic_toric_audit() -> dict[str, object]:
   329	    time, phi, xi1, xi2 = sp.symbols("t phi xi1 xi2", real=True)
   330	    coordinates = (time, phi, xi1, xi2)
   331	    radial = sp.Function("A", positive=True)(phi)
   332	    common = sp.Function("Omega", positive=True)(phi)
   333	    metric = sp.diag(
   334	        -1,
   335	        radial**2,
   336	        common**2 * sp.exp(-2 * phi),
   337	        common**2 * sp.exp(2 * phi),
   338	    )
   339	    inverse = sp.simplify(metric.inv())
   340	    gamma = [[[
   341	        sp.simplify(sum(
   342	            inverse[upper, lower] * (
   343	                sp.diff(metric[lower, right], coordinates[left])
   344	                + sp.diff(metric[lower, left], coordinates[right])
   345	                - sp.diff(metric[left, right], coordinates[lower])
   346	            )
   347	            for lower in range(4)
   348	        ) / 2)
   349	        for right in range(4)] for left in range(4)] for upper in range(4)]
   350	    hessian = sp.Matrix(
   351	        4, 4,
   352	        lambda upper, lower: sp.simplify(
   353	            -sum(inverse[upper, index] * gamma[1][index][lower] for index in range(4))
   354	        ),
   355	    )
   356	    dyad = sp.zeros(4)
   357	    dyad[1, 1] = inverse[1, 1]
   358	    expected_hessian = sp.diag(
   359	        0,
   360	        -sp.diff(radial, phi) / radial**3,
   361	        (sp.diff(common, phi) / common - 1) / radial**2,
   362	        (sp.diff(common, phi) / common + 1) / radial**2,
   363	    )
   364	    expected_dyad = sp.diag(0, radial**-2, 0, 0)
   365	    hessian_residual = sp.simplify(hessian - expected_hessian)
   366	    dyad_residual = sp.simplify(dyad - expected_dyad)
   367	    angular_gap = sp.simplify(hessian[3, 3] - hessian[2, 2])
   368	
   369	    diagonal_generator = sp.Matrix((0, 0, 1, 1))
   370	    generator_flat = metric * diagonal_generator
   371	    generator_norm = sp.simplify((diagonal_generator.T * metric * diagonal_generator)[0])
   372	    connection = [sp.simplify(value / generator_norm) for value in generator_flat]
   373	    weight = sp.simplify(connection[2])
   374	    expected_weight = sp.simplify(1 / (1 + sp.exp(4 * phi)))
   375	    connection_residual = sp.simplify((weight - expected_weight).rewrite(sp.exp))
   376	    quotient = sp.Matrix((
   377	        sp.sech(2 * phi) * sp.cos(xi1 - xi2),
   378	        sp.sech(2 * phi) * sp.sin(xi1 - xi2),
   379	        -sp.tanh(2 * phi),
   380	    ))
   381	    quotient_norm_residual = sp.simplify((quotient.dot(quotient) - 1).rewrite(sp.exp))
   382	    unit_limit = sp.simplify(
   383	        sp.limit(weight, phi, -sp.oo) - sp.limit(weight, phi, sp.oo)
   384	    )
   385	    if hessian_residual != sp.zeros(4) or dyad_residual != sp.zeros(4):
   386	        raise AssertionError("symbolic metric derivation")
   387	    if sp.simplify(angular_gap - 2 / radial**2) != 0:
   388	        raise AssertionError("symbolic angular gap")
   389	    if connection_residual != 0 or quotient_norm_residual != 0 or unit_limit != 1:
   390	        raise AssertionError("symbolic connection/quotient")
   391	    return {
   392	        "christoffels_derived_from_metric": True,
   393	        "mixed_hessian_derived_from_metric": True,
   394	        "gradient_dyad_derived_from_metric": True,
   395	        "angular_gap": str(angular_gap),
   396	        "diagonal_connection_weight": str(weight),
   397	        "connection_common_scale_cancelled": not weight.has(common),
   398	        "quotient_norm_exact": quotient_norm_residual == 0,
   399	        "conditional_full_range_unit_limit": str(unit_limit),
   400	    }
   401	
   402	
   403	def direct_hopf_seed_audit() -> dict[str, object]:
   404	    source = ROOT / "hopfion_arc_scripts_2026-07-05/fs_hopfion.py"
   405	    tree = ast.parse(source.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
   406	    if not any(isinstance(node, ast.FunctionDef) and node.name == "hopf_seed" for node in tree.body):
   407	        raise AssertionError("hopf_seed function absent")
   408	    specification = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("frozen_hopf_seed_module", source)
   409	    if specification is None or specification.loader is None:
   410	        raise AssertionError("hopf_seed import specification")
   411	    module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(specification)
   412	    specification.loader.exec_module(module)
   413	    import torch
   414	
   415	    if module.dev != "cpu":
   416	        raise AssertionError("CPU-only seed replay")
   417	    generator = np.random.default_rng(20260722)
   418	    phi = generator.uniform(-2.0, 2.0, 1000)
   419	    xi1 = generator.uniform(-math.pi, math.pi, 1000)
   420	    xi2 = generator.uniform(-math.pi, math.pi, 1000)
   421	    eta = np.arctan(np.exp(2 * phi))
   422	    s1 = np.cos(eta) * np.cos(xi1)
   423	    s2 = np.cos(eta) * np.sin(xi1)
   424	    s3 = np.sin(eta) * np.cos(xi2)
   425	    s4 = np.sin(eta) * np.sin(xi2)
   426	    scale = 1.7
   427	    denominator = 1 + s4
   428	    x = scale * s1 / denominator
   429	    y = scale * s2 / denominator
   430	    z = scale * s3 / denominator
   431	    with torch.no_grad():
   432	        actual = module.hopf_seed(
   433	            torch.as_tensor(x, dtype=torch.float64),
   434	            torch.as_tensor(y, dtype=torch.float64),
   435	            torch.as_tensor(z, dtype=torch.float64),
   436	            scale,
   437	        ).cpu().numpy()
   438	    delta = xi1 - xi2
   439	    expected = np.asarray((
   440	        np.cosh(2 * phi) ** -1 * np.cos(delta),
   441	        np.cosh(2 * phi) ** -1 * np.sin(delta),
   442	        -np.tanh(2 * phi),
   443	    ))
   444	    residual = float(np.max(np.abs(actual - expected)))
   445	    return {
   446	        "source_path": str(source.relative_to(ROOT)),
   447	        "source_sha256": digest(source),
   448	        "function_executed": "hopf_seed",
   449	        "device": module.dev,
   450	        "dtype": "float64",
   451	        "sample_points": 1000,
   452	        "sample_seed": 20260722,
   453	        "maximum_absolute_residual": residual,
   454	    }
   455	
   456	
   457	def validate_source_lineage(rows: list[dict[str, str]]) -> None:
   458	    if len(rows) != 10 or len({row["path"] for row in rows}) != 10:
   459	        raise AssertionError("complete source lineage")
   460	    indexed = {row["path"]: row["sha256"] for row in rows}
   461	    for relative, expected in DIRECT_SOURCES.items():
   462	        if indexed.get(relative) != expected:
   463	            raise AssertionError(f"direct source lineage {relative}")
   464	        if digest(ROOT / relative) != expected:
   465	            raise AssertionError(f"direct source manifest identity {relative}")
   466	        package = ROOT / Path(relative).parent
   467	        for line in (package / "SHA256SUMS.txt").read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
   468	            if not line.strip():
   469	                continue
   470	            wanted, name = line.split(maxsplit=1)
   471	            if digest(package / name.strip()) != wanted:
   472	                raise AssertionError(f"direct source manifest content {relative}:{name}")
   473	
   474	
   475	def validate_result(result: dict[str, object], lineage: list[dict[str, str]]) -> None:
   476	    covariance = result["covariance"]
   477	    symbolic = result["symbolic_toric"]
   478	    seed = result["direct_hopf_seed"]
   479	    provenance = result["construction_provenance"]
   480	    if covariance["blind_identities"] != 64 or covariance["stored_nonlinear_transforms"] != 2:
   481	        raise AssertionError("covariance anchor coverage")
   482	    if covariance["all_family_node_comparisons"] != 64 * 17 * 31 * 2:
   483	        raise AssertionError("covariance family/node coverage")
   484	    point_status = covariance["point_status_census"]
   485	    if set(point_status) != {"BOTH_CLASSIFIED", "ONE_SIDED_UNCERTAIN", "BOTH_UNCERTAIN"}:
   486	        raise AssertionError("point status classes")
   487	    if sum(point_status.values()) != covariance["all_family_node_comparisons"]:
   488	        raise AssertionError("point status completeness")
   489	    if covariance["uncertainty_bearing_point_comparisons"] != (
   490	        point_status["ONE_SIDED_UNCERTAIN"] + point_status["BOTH_UNCERTAIN"]
   491	    ):
   492	        raise AssertionError("uncertainty accounting")
   493	    if covariance["nonuncertain_classification_discordances"] != 0:
   494	        raise AssertionError("coordinate classification discordance")
   495	    if covariance["coordinate_map_interpretation"] != MAP_INTERPRETATION:
   496	        raise AssertionError("node-dependent nonlinear coordinate map")
   497	    if covariance["coordinate_map_evidence_status"] != "CONFIRMATORY_POST_SECOND_REVIEW_REPAIR":
   498	        raise AssertionError("coordinate map evidence provenance")
   499	    if covariance["maximum_inverse_map_residual"] > 1.0e-11:
   500	        raise AssertionError("coordinate map inverse residual")
   501	    if covariance["minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant"] <= 1.0e-6:
   502	        raise AssertionError("coordinate map Jacobian degeneracy")
   503	    if covariance["maximum_intrinsic_object_covariance_residual"] > COVARIANCE_TOLERANCE:
   504	        raise AssertionError("intrinsic object covariance residual")
   505	    if covariance["maximum_projector_set_covariance_residual"] > COVARIANCE_TOLERANCE:
   506	        raise AssertionError("projector covariance residual")
   507	    if covariance["possible_edge_transport_comparisons"] != 64 * 16 * 31 * 2:
   508	        raise AssertionError("possible edge coverage")
   509	    if covariance["matched_edge_transport_comparisons"] <= 0:
   510	        raise AssertionError("missing matched edge coverage")
   511	    if covariance["matched_edge_transport_comparisons"] + covariance["skipped_edge_transport_comparisons"] != covariance["possible_edge_transport_comparisons"]:
   512	        raise AssertionError("edge comparison accounting")
   513	    if sum(covariance["skipped_edge_reason_census"].values()) != covariance["skipped_edge_transport_comparisons"]:
   514	        raise AssertionError("skipped edge reason accounting")
   515	    if covariance["matched_edge_transport_discordances"] != 0:
   516	        raise AssertionError("path matching covariance")
   517	    if result["frobenius_certification_scope"] != "REGISTERED_CHART_ONLY":
   518	        raise AssertionError("Frobenius scope promotion")
   519	    required_symbolic = (
   520	        "christoffels_derived_from_metric", "mixed_hessian_derived_from_metric",
   521	        "gradient_dyad_derived_from_metric", "connection_common_scale_cancelled",
   522	        "quotient_norm_exact",
   523	    )
   524	    if not all(symbolic[key] is True for key in required_symbolic):
   525	        raise AssertionError("symbolic toric derivation")
   526	    if symbolic["angular_gap"] != "2/A(phi)**2":
   527	        raise AssertionError("symbolic angular gap")
   528	    if symbolic["diagonal_connection_weight"] != "exp(-2*phi)/(2*cosh(2*phi))":
   529	        raise AssertionError("symbolic connection weight")
   530	    if symbolic["conditional_full_range_unit_limit"] != "1":
   531	        raise AssertionError("symbolic unit limit")
   532	    if seed["function_executed"] != "hopf_seed" or seed["device"] != "cpu":
   533	        raise AssertionError("direct seed execution")
   534	    if seed["source_sha256"] != HOPF_SEED_SHA256:
   535	        raise AssertionError("direct seed source identity")
   536	    if seed["dtype"] != "float64" or seed["sample_points"] != 1000 or seed["sample_seed"] != 20260722:
   537	        raise AssertionError("direct seed sample contract")
   538	    if seed["maximum_absolute_residual"] > SEED_TOLERANCE:
   539	        raise AssertionError("direct seed residual")
   540	    if provenance != {
   541	        "supplied_equal_weight_circle_action": True,
   542	        "imported_s2_matter_carrier": False,
   543	        "imported_l2_l4_action_functional": False,
   544	    }:
   545	        raise AssertionError("construction provenance")
   546	    if result["overall_correspondence_status"] != "LEAD":
   547	        raise AssertionError("correspondence promotion")
   548	    if result["sampled_path_status"] != SAMPLED_STATUS:
   549	        raise AssertionError("sampled path promotion")
   550	    if result["maximum_conclusion"] != MAXIMUM:
   551	        raise AssertionError("maximum conclusion")
   552	    validate_source_lineage(lineage)
   553

   555	def mutation_catches(
   556	    result: dict[str, object], lineage: list[dict[str, str]]
   557	) -> list[dict[str, str]]:
   558	    mutations = []
   559	
   560	    def add(name: str, mutate) -> None:
   561	        candidate = copy.deepcopy(result)
   562	        candidate_lineage = copy.deepcopy(lineage)
   563	        mutate(candidate, candidate_lineage)

   565	            validate_result(candidate, candidate_lineage)
   566	        except AssertionError:
   567	            mutations.append({"catch_id": name, "result": "MUTATION_REJECTED"})
   568	            return
   569	        raise AssertionError(f"mutation survived {name}")
   570	
   571	    add("K01_MISSING_COVARIANCE_COMPARISON", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(

   643	def main() -> None:
   644	    covariance = covariance_audit()
   645	    symbolic = symbolic_toric_audit()
   646	    seed = direct_hopf_seed_audit()
   647	    result = {
   648	        "schema": "udt-motif-hopf-review-correction-1.0",
   649	        "status": "PASS_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE",
   650	        "covariance": covariance,
   651	        "frobenius_certification_scope": "REGISTERED_CHART_ONLY",
   652	        "symbolic_toric": symbolic,
   653	        "direct_hopf_seed": seed,
   654	        "construction_provenance": {
   655	            "supplied_equal_weight_circle_action": True,
   656	            "imported_s2_matter_carrier": False,
   657	            "imported_l2_l4_action_functional": False,
   658	        },
   659	        "sampled_path_status": SAMPLED_STATUS,
   660	        "overall_correspondence_status": "LEAD",
   661	        "maximum_conclusion": MAXIMUM,
   662	    }
   663	    lineage = read_tsv(HERE / "SOURCE_LINEAGE.tsv")
   664	    validate_result(result, lineage)
   665	    catches = mutation_catches(result, lineage)
   666	    result["exercised_mutation_catches"] = len(catches)
   667	    with (HERE / "REVIEW_CORRECTION_CATCH_PROOFS.tsv").open(
   668	        "w", encoding="utf-8", newline=""
   669	    ) as handle:
   670	        writer = csv.DictWriter(
   671	            handle, fieldnames=("catch_id", "result"), delimiter="\t", lineterminator="\n"
   672	        )
   673	        writer.writeheader()
   674	        writer.writerows(catches)
   675	    (HERE / "REVIEW_CORRECTION_RESULT.json").write_text(
   676	        json.dumps(result, indent=2, sort_keys=True) + "\n", encoding="utf-8"
   677	    )
   678	    print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, sort_keys=True))

   682	    main()

    54	@dataclass
    55	class Jet:
    56	    value: float
    57	    first: np.ndarray
    58	    second: np.ndarray
    59	
    60	    @classmethod
    61	    def constant(cls, value):
    62	        return cls(float(value), np.zeros(4), np.zeros((4, 4)))
    63	
    64	    def __add__(self, other):
    65	        rhs = other if isinstance(other, Jet) else Jet.constant(other)
    66	        return Jet(self.value + rhs.value, self.first + rhs.first, self.second + rhs.second)
    67	
    68	    __radd__ = __add__
    69	
    70	    def __neg__(self):
    71	        return Jet(-self.value, -self.first, -self.second)
    72	
    73	    def __sub__(self, other):
    74	        return self + (-other if isinstance(other, Jet) else -other)
    75	
    76	    def __rsub__(self, other):
    77	        return (-self) + other
    78	
    79	    def __mul__(self, other):
    80	        rhs = other if isinstance(other, Jet) else Jet.constant(other)
    81	        return Jet(
    82	            self.value * rhs.value,
    83	            self.first * rhs.value + self.value * rhs.first,
    84	            self.second * rhs.value + self.value * rhs.second
    85	            + np.outer(self.first, rhs.first) + np.outer(rhs.first, self.first),
    86	        )
    87	
    88	    __rmul__ = __mul__
    89	
    90	
    91	def jexp(value: Jet) -> Jet:
    92	    current = math.exp(value.value)
    93	    return Jet(current, current * value.first, current * (value.second + np.outer(value.first, value.first)))
    94	
    95	
    96	def features(x: np.ndarray) -> list[Jet]:
    97	    rows = []
    98	    for coordinate in range(4):
    99	        first = np.zeros(4); first[coordinate] = 1
   100	        rows.append(Jet(float(x[coordinate]), first, np.zeros((4, 4))))
   101	    for coordinate in range(4):
   102	        first = np.zeros(4); first[coordinate] = x[coordinate]
   103	        second = np.zeros((4, 4)); second[coordinate, coordinate] = 1
   104	        rows.append(Jet(0.5 * float(x[coordinate] ** 2), first, second))
   105	    for a, b in independent.PAIRS:
   106	        first = np.zeros(4); first[a] = x[b]; first[b] = x[a]
   107	        second = np.zeros((4, 4)); second[a, b] = second[b, a] = 1
   108	        rows.append(Jet(float(x[a] * x[b]), first, second))
   109	    return rows

   111	
   112	def coefficient(bank: int, field: int, term: int) -> float:
   113	    raw = ((bank + 2) * 11 + (field + 1) * 7 + (term + 1) * 5 + (bank + 1) * (field + term + 3)) % 19 - 9
   114	    if raw == 0:
   115	        raw = 1 if (bank + field + term) % 2 == 0 else -1
   116	    return raw / (60.0 if term < 4 else 90.0 if term < 8 else 120.0)
   117	
   118	
   119	def polynomial(bank: int, field: int, x: np.ndarray) -> Jet:
   120	    result = Jet.constant(0)
   121	    for term, feature in enumerate(features(x)):
   122	        result += coefficient(bank, field, term) * feature
   123	    return result

   125	
   126	def metric_phi_jets(bank: int, amplitudes: np.ndarray, x: np.ndarray):
   127	    latent = [Jet.constant(BASE_VALUES[index]) + amplitudes[index] * polynomial(bank, index, x) for index in range(10)]
   128	    a, b, c, d, e, f, a20, a30, a21, a31 = latent
   129	    u, w, r, t = jexp(a), jexp(c), jexp(d), jexp(f)
   130	    slots = (-(u*u), -(u*b), w*w-b*b, r*r, r*e, e*e+t*t, a20, a30, a21, a31)
   131	    h = [[slots[0], slots[1]], [slots[1], slots[2]]]
   132	    q = [[slots[3], slots[4]], [slots[4], slots[5]]]
   133	    shifts = [[slots[6], slots[8]], [slots[7], slots[9]]]
   134	    zero = Jet.constant(0)
   135	    metric = [[zero for _ in range(4)] for _ in range(4)]
   136	    for i in range(2):
   137	        for j in range(2):
   138	            metric[i][j] = h[i][j] + sum((q[a0][b0] * shifts[a0][i] * shifts[b0][j]
   139	                                           for a0 in range(2) for b0 in range(2)), Jet.constant(0))
   140	        for b0 in range(2):
   141	            metric[i][2+b0] = sum((q[a0][b0] * shifts[a0][i] for a0 in range(2)), Jet.constant(0))
   142	            metric[2+b0][i] = metric[i][2+b0]
   143	    for a0 in range(2):
   144	        for b0 in range(2):
   145	            metric[2+a0][2+b0] = q[a0][b0]
   146	    g = np.asarray([[metric[mu][nu].value for nu in range(4)] for mu in range(4)])
   147	    dg = np.asarray([[[metric[mu][nu].first[k] for nu in range(4)] for mu in range(4)] for k in range(4)])
   148	    ddg = np.asarray([[[[metric[mu][nu].second[k, ell] for nu in range(4)] for mu in range(4)]
   149	                        for ell in range(4)] for k in range(4)])
   150	    phi = Jet.constant(PHI_OFFSETS[bank]) + amplitudes[10] * polynomial(bank, 10, x)
   151	    return g, dg, ddg, phi.first, phi.second

   177	def classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point, selected_masks=None):
   178	    g, dg, ddg, dphi, ddphi = metric_phi_jets(bank, amplitudes, point)
   179	    objects, geo = independent.objects(g, dg, ddg, dphi, ddphi)
   180	    scalar = {key: objects[key] for key in ("R", "H", "D")}
   181	    results = {}
   182	    for family_id, mask, keys in FAMILIES:
   183	        if selected_masks is not None and mask not in selected_masks:
   184	            continue
   185	        results[mask] = independent.classify(independent.operators(objects, keys), objects["gradient"], g, scalar, keys)
   186	    return geo, results

   189	def path_points(bank):
   190	    start_id, end_id = POINT_PAIRS[bank]
   191	    start = np.asarray(POINTS[start_id]); end = np.asarray(POINTS[end_id])
   192	    return [(1-t)*start+t*end for t in (node/16 for node in range(17))]

   195	def labels(result):
   196	    return [(int(row["rank"]), str(row["signature"])) for row in result["blocks"]]
   197	
   198	
   199	def match(reference, current):
   200	    first_labels, second_labels = labels(reference), labels(current)
   201	    if Counter(first_labels) != Counter(second_labels):
   202	        return None
   203	    first, second = reference["projectors"], current["projectors"]
   204	    best = None; distance = math.inf
   205	    for permutation in itertools.permutations(range(len(second))):
   206	        if any(first_labels[index] != second_labels[permutation[index]] for index in range(len(first))):
   207	            continue
   208	        ordered = [second[permutation[index]] for index in range(len(first))]
   209	        current_distance = max((independent.relmax(first[index], ordered[index]) for index in range(len(first))), default=0)
   210	        if current_distance < distance:
   211	            best, distance = ordered, current_distance
   212	    return best
   213	
   214	
   215	def covariant_derivative(projector, partial, gamma):
   216	    output = np.asarray(partial).copy()
   217	    for rho, nu, beta, sigma in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=4):
   218	        output[rho,nu,beta] += gamma[nu,rho,sigma]*projector[sigma,beta] - gamma[sigma,rho,beta]*projector[nu,sigma]
   219	    return output
   220	
   221	
   222	def frobenius(projector, partial, gamma):
   223	    nabla = covariant_derivative(projector, partial, gamma); term = np.zeros((4,4,4))
   224	    for nu, alpha, beta, rho in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=4):
   225	        term[nu,alpha,beta] += projector[rho,alpha]*nabla[rho,nu,beta] - projector[rho,beta]*nabla[rho,nu,alpha]
   226	    value = np.einsum("mn,nab->mab", np.eye(4)-projector, term)
   227	    return float(np.linalg.norm(value)/max(np.linalg.norm(nabla),1e-30))
   228	
   229	
   230	def frob_class(value, convergence):
   231	    if convergence > DERIVATIVE_GATE: return "NUMERIC_UNCERTAIN_DERIVATIVE"
   232	    if value <= FROB_LOW: return "NUMERICALLY_INTEGRABLE_LOCAL"
   233	    if value >= FROB_HIGH: return "NUMERICALLY_NONINTEGRABLE_LOCAL"
   234	    return "NUMERIC_UNCERTAIN_OBSTRUCTION"
   235	
   236	
   237	def distribution_multiset(bank, amplitudes, mask):
   238	    points = path_points(bank); midpoint = points[8]
   239	    geo, center_results = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, midpoint, {mask}); center = center_results[mask]
   240	    stencil = {}
   241	    for step in H_STEPS:
   242	        for axis in range(4):
   243	            for sign in (-1,1):
   244	                point = midpoint.copy(); point[axis] += sign*step
   245	                _, current = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point, {mask}); stencil[(step,axis,sign)] = current[mask]
   246	    all_results = [center, *stencil.values()]
   247	    stable = center["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED" and all(
   248	        current["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED" and Counter(labels(current)) == Counter(labels(center))
   249	        for current in all_results
   250	    )
   251	    if not stable:
   252	        return Counter({("UNRESOLVED", "-", "NOT_CLASSIFIED"): 1}), False
   253	    center_projectors = [np.asarray(item) for item in center["projectors"]]; derivatives = {}
   254	    for step in H_STEPS:
   255	        current_derivatives = [np.zeros((4,4,4)) for _ in center_projectors]
   256	        for axis in range(4):
   257	            minus = match(center, stencil[(step,axis,-1)]); plus = match(center, stencil[(step,axis,1)])
   258	            if minus is None or plus is None:
   259	                return Counter({("UNRESOLVED", "-", "NOT_CLASSIFIED"): 1}), False
   260	            for index in range(len(center_projectors)):
   261	                current_derivatives[index][axis] = (plus[index]-minus[index])/(2*step)
   262	        derivatives[step] = current_derivatives
   263	    candidates = []
   264	    for index, block in enumerate(center["blocks"]):
   265	        candidates.append(("PRIMITIVE_BLOCK", [index], int(block["rank"])))
   266	    for pair in independent.splits(center_projectors):
   267	        for projector in pair:
   268	            members = [index for index,item in enumerate(center_projectors) if independent.relmax(projector@item,item) <= 1e-8]
   269	            candidates.append(("COMPLEMENTARY_RANK2", members, 2))
   270	    census = Counter(); gamma = np.asarray(geo["gamma"])
   271	    for kind, members, rank in candidates:
   272	        projector = sum((center_projectors[index] for index in members), np.zeros((4,4)))
   273	        dh = sum((derivatives[H_STEPS[0]][index] for index in members), np.zeros((4,4,4)))
   274	        dh2 = sum((derivatives[H_STEPS[1]][index] for index in members), np.zeros((4,4,4)))
   275	        convergence = float(np.linalg.norm(dh-dh2)/max(np.linalg.norm(dh2),1.0))
   276	        if rank == 1: classification = "LOCALLY_INTEGRABLE_BY_RANK_ONE"
   277	        elif rank == 4: classification = "WHOLE_TANGENT_SPACE"
   278	        else: classification = frob_class(frobenius(projector,dh2,gamma),convergence)
   279	        census[(kind,str(rank),classification)] += 1
   280	    return census, True
   281	
   282	
   283	def exact_toric_check():
   284	    phi = sp.symbols("phi", real=True); A, Ap, O, Op = sp.symbols("A Ap O Op", positive=True)
   285	    h = (0, -Ap/A**3, (Op/O-1)/A**2, (Op/O+1)/A**2); d = (0,1/A**2,0,0)
   286	    if sp.simplify(h[3]-h[2]-2/A**2) != 0: raise AssertionError("toric angular gap")
   287	    f = sp.simplify(1/(1+sp.exp(4*phi)))
   288	    q = sp.simplify(sp.limit(f,phi,-sp.oo)-sp.limit(f,phi,sp.oo))
   289	    n2 = sp.simplify((sp.sech(2*phi)**2+sp.tanh(2*phi)**2).rewrite(sp.exp))
   290	    if q != 1 or n2 != 1: raise AssertionError("toric unit/norm")
   291	    round_b = sp.simplify(sp.exp(-2*phi)/(2*sp.cosh(2*phi))); round_c = sp.simplify(sp.exp(2*phi)/(2*sp.cosh(2*phi)))
   292	    caps = (sp.limit(round_b,phi,-sp.oo),sp.limit(round_b,phi,sp.oo),sp.limit(round_c,phi,-sp.oo),sp.limit(round_c,phi,sp.oo))
   293	    if caps != (1,0,0,1): raise AssertionError("round caps")
   294	    return {"angular_gap": str(sp.simplify(h[3]-h[2])), "conditional_unit_q": str(q), "quotient_norm": str(n2), "round_caps": list(map(str,caps))}
   295	
   296	
   297	def main():
   298	    identity_lookup = identity_data(); ids = sorted(identity_lookup, key=lambda value: hashlib.sha256(("MOTIF_HOPF_INDEPENDENT_V1|"+value).encode()).hexdigest())[:64]
   299	    if len(ids) != 64: raise AssertionError("blind anchors")
   300	    blind = {}
   301	    for identity_id in ids:
   302	        bank, amplitudes = identity_lookup[identity_id]
   303	        for node, point in enumerate(path_points(bank)):
   304	            _, results = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point)
   305	            for family_id, mask, _keys in FAMILIES:
   306	                blind[(identity_id,node,family_id)] = results[mask]
   307	    if len(blind) != 64*17*31: raise AssertionError("blind coverage")
   308	
   309	    summaries = list(gzip_rows(HERE/"PATH_CONTINUATION_SUMMARY.tsv.gz"))
   310	    adverse = {(row["identity_id"],row["family_id"],int(row["family_mask"])) for row in summaries
   311	               if int(row["motif_transitions"]) or int(row["classified_nodes"]) != 17}
   312	    adverse_results = {}
   313	    for identity_id, family_id, mask in sorted(adverse):
   314	        bank, amplitudes = identity_lookup[identity_id]
   315	        for node, point in enumerate(path_points(bank)):
   316	            _, current = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point, {mask})
   317	            adverse_results[(identity_id,node,family_id)] = current[mask]
   318	
   319	    wanted = set(blind) | set(adverse_results); saved = {}
   320	    for row in gzip_rows(HERE/"PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
   321	        key=(row["identity_id"],int(row["path_node"]),row["family_id"])
   322	        if key in wanted: saved[key]=row
   323	    if len(saved) != len(wanted): raise AssertionError("saved comparison coverage")
   324	    mismatches=[]
   325	    for source in (blind,adverse_results):
   326	        for key,current in source.items():
   327	            row=saved[key]
   328	            for field in COMPARE:
   329	                if str(current[field]) != row[field]: mismatches.append((key,field,str(current[field]),row[field]))
   330	    if mismatches: raise AssertionError(f"classification mismatches {mismatches[:3]}")
   331	
   332	    saved_distribution = defaultdict(Counter); unstable_saved=set()
   333	    for row in gzip_rows(HERE/"DISTRIBUTION_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
   334	        key=(row["identity_id"],row["family_id"],int(row["family_mask"]))
   335	        if row["stencil_status"] != "STABLE_CLASSIFIED": unstable_saved.add(key)
   336	        if row["identity_id"] in ids:
   337	            saved_distribution[key][(row["distribution_kind"],row["rank"],row["frobenius_class"])] += 1
   338	    distribution_comparisons=0
   339	    for identity_id in ids:
   340	        bank, amplitudes=identity_lookup[identity_id]
   341	        for family_id,mask,_keys in FAMILIES:
   342	            got,_stable=distribution_multiset(bank,amplitudes,mask); key=(identity_id,family_id,mask)
   343	            if got != saved_distribution[key]: raise AssertionError(f"distribution mismatch {key} {got} {saved_distribution[key]}")
   344	            distribution_comparisons += sum(got.values())
   345	    if len(unstable_saved) != 13: raise AssertionError("unstable saved count")
   346	    unstable_reproduced=0
   347	    for identity_id,family_id,mask in sorted(unstable_saved):
   348	        bank,amplitudes=identity_lookup[identity_id]; _got,stable=distribution_multiset(bank,amplitudes,mask)
   349	        unstable_reproduced += not stable
   350	    if unstable_reproduced != 13: raise AssertionError("unstable stencil reproduction")
   351	
   352	    toric=exact_toric_check(); catches=[]
   353	    def catch(name, condition):
   354	        if not condition: raise AssertionError(f"catch failed {name}")
   355	        catches.append({"catch_id":name,"result":"REJECTED_AS_REQUIRED"})
   356	    catch("K01_MISSING_BLIND_ANCHOR", len(ids[:-1]) != 64)
   357	    catch("K02_MISSING_PATH_NODE", len(range(16)) != 17)
   358	    catch("K03_MISSING_FAMILY", len(FAMILIES[:-1]) != 31)
   359	    catch("K04_MUTATED_COEFFICIENT", coefficient(0,0,0) != coefficient(0,0,0)+1e-3)
   360	    # The covariant Hessian differs from the partial Hessian on a curved blind anchor.
   361	    identity_id=ids[0]; bank,amps=identity_lookup[identity_id]; point=path_points(bank)[8]
   362	    g,dg,ddg,pf,ps=metric_phi_jets(bank,amps,point); obj,geo=independent.objects(g,dg,ddg,pf,ps)
   363	    catch("K05_OMITTED_HESSIAN_CONNECTION", independent.relmax(obj["H"],np.linalg.inv(g)@ps) > independent.TOL)
   364	    catch("K06_PROJECTOR_PERMUTATION", independent.set_distance([np.diag((1,0,0,0)),np.diag((0,1,1,1))],[np.diag((0,1,1,1)),np.diag((1,0,0,0))]) <= independent.TOL)
   365	    catch("K07_MANUFACTURED_GLOBAL_ELIGIBILITY", json.loads((HERE/"ATLAS_RESULT.json").read_text())["global_hopf_eligible_local_identities"] == 0)
   366	    catch("K08_FORCED_FINITE_ENDPOINT_Q", abs((0.8-0.2)-1.0) > 0.1)
   367	    toric_saved=json.loads((HERE/"TORIC_CONTROL_RESULT.json").read_text())
   368	    catch("K09_OMITTED_CIRCLE_ACTION", "selected free diagonal or anti-diagonal circle action" in toric_saved["global_premises_for_unit_class"])
   369	    catch("K10_FALSE_SEED_RELAXED_IDENTITY", toric_saved["maximum_conclusion"] != "NATIVE_RELAXED_HOPFION_DERIVED")
   370	    catch(
   371	        "K11_CONSTRUCTION_PROVENANCE_DISCLOSED",
   372	        toric_saved["supplied_equal_weight_circle_action"] is True
   373	        and toric_saved["construction_used_s2_matter_carrier"] is False
   374	        and toric_saved["construction_used_l2_l4_action_functional"] is False,
   375	    )
   376	    with (HERE/"INDEPENDENT_CATCH_PROOFS.tsv").open("w",encoding="utf-8",newline="") as handle:
   377	        writer=csv.DictWriter(handle,fieldnames=("catch_id","result"),delimiter="\t",lineterminator="\n"); writer.writeheader(); writer.writerows(catches)
   378	    result={
   379	        "status":"PASS_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE", "blind_anchor_identities":64,
   380	        "blind_path_family_comparisons":len(blind), "adverse_path_family_comparisons":len(adverse_results),
   381	        "adverse_family_paths":len(adverse), "classification_mismatches":0,
   382	        "blind_distribution_rows_compared":distribution_comparisons,
   383	        "unstable_stencils_reproduced":unstable_reproduced,
   384	        "toric_control_regression":toric,
   385	        "toric_independence_status":"REGRESSION_ONLY_SUPERSEDED_BY_REVIEW_CORRECTION",
   386	        "legacy_declaration_catches":len(catches),
   387	        "independent_implementation":"frozen nonproduction motif algebra plus independent analytic Jet reconstruction",
   388	        "maximum_conclusion":"BOUNDED_ANALYTIC_PATH_AND_REGISTERED_CHART_DISTRIBUTION_REPLAY",
   389	    }
   390	    (HERE/"INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION_RESULT.json").write_text(json.dumps(result,indent=2,sort_keys=True)+"\n",encoding="utf-8")
   391	    print(json.dumps(result,indent=2,sort_keys=True))
   392

   394	if __name__ == "__main__":
   395	    main()

    27	def digest(path):
    28	    value=hashlib.sha256()
    29	    with Path(path).open("rb") as handle:
    30	        for block in iter(lambda:handle.read(131072),b""): value.update(block)
    31	    return value.hexdigest()

    34	def rows(path):
    35	    with gzip.open(path,"rt",encoding="utf-8",newline="") as handle: yield from csv.DictReader(handle,delimiter="\t")

    38	def validate_counts(identity_rows,path_count,summary_count):
    39	    if identity_rows != EXPECTED["identities"]: raise AssertionError("identity count")
    40	    if path_count != EXPECTED["path_rows"]: raise AssertionError("path count")
    41	    if summary_count != EXPECTED["summaries"]: raise AssertionError("summary count")
    42	
    43	
    44	def validate_global_status(result):
    45	    if result["global_hopf_eligible_local_identities"] != 0: raise AssertionError("manufactured global eligibility")
    46	    if result["global_status"] != "GLOBAL_DATA_ABSENT_FOR_ALL_LOCAL_ANALYTIC_IDENTITIES": raise AssertionError("global status")
    47	
    48	
    49	def validate_toric(toric):
    50	    if toric["conditional_unit_q"] != "1": raise AssertionError("unit control")
    51	    if toric["hopf_q_finite_endpoints"] != "f_minus - f_plus": raise AssertionError("finite endpoint law")
    52	    if toric["supplied_equal_weight_circle_action"] is not True: raise AssertionError("circle action disclosure")
    53	    if toric["construction_used_s2_matter_carrier"] is not False: raise AssertionError("S2 carrier import")
    54	    if toric["construction_used_l2_l4_action_functional"] is not False: raise AssertionError("L2+L4 import")
    55	    if "selected free diagonal or anti-diagonal circle action" not in toric["global_premises_for_unit_class"]: raise AssertionError("circle action premise")
    56	    if toric["maximum_conclusion"] == "NATIVE_RELAXED_HOPFION_DERIVED": raise AssertionError("seed/relaxed promotion")

    59	def main():
    60	    result=json.loads((HERE/"ATLAS_RESULT.json").read_text()); toric=json.loads((HERE/"TORIC_CONTROL_RESULT.json").read_text())
    61	    independent=json.loads((HERE/"INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION_RESULT.json").read_text())
    62	    correction=json.loads((HERE/"REVIEW_CORRECTION_RESULT.json").read_text())
    63	    correction_verifier.validate_result(
    64	        correction, correction_verifier.read_tsv(HERE/"SOURCE_LINEAGE.tsv")
    65	    )
    66	    identity_rows=sum(1 for _ in (HERE/"COHERENT_IDENTITY_REGISTRY.tsv").open())-1
    67	    path_count=sum(1 for _ in rows(HERE/"PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz")); summary_count=sum(1 for _ in rows(HERE/"PATH_CONTINUATION_SUMMARY.tsv.gz"))
    68	    validate_counts(identity_rows,path_count,summary_count); validate_global_status(result); validate_toric(toric)
    69	    if independent["status"] != "PASS_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE" or independent["classification_mismatches"] != 0: raise AssertionError("independent verifier")
    70	    if correction["status"] != "PASS_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE" or correction["maximum_conclusion"] != MAXIMUM: raise AssertionError("review correction")
    71	    if correction["covariance"]["all_family_node_comparisons"] != 67456: raise AssertionError("covariance coverage")
    72	    if correction["covariance"]["nonuncertain_classification_discordances"] != 0: raise AssertionError("covariance classification")
    73	    if correction["covariance"]["matched_edge_transport_discordances"] != 0: raise AssertionError("edge transport covariance")
    74	    if correction["frobenius_certification_scope"] != "REGISTERED_CHART_ONLY": raise AssertionError("Frobenius scope")
    75	    if correction["exercised_mutation_catches"] != 23: raise AssertionError("correction catches")
    76	    for name in ("PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz","PATH_CONTINUATION_SUMMARY.tsv.gz","DISTRIBUTION_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
    77	        with (HERE/name).open("rb") as handle: header=handle.read(10)
    78	        if struct.unpack("<I",header[4:8])[0] != 0: raise AssertionError(f"nondeterministic gzip {name}")
    79	
    80	    prior={}
    81	    for row in rows(MOTIF/"FAMILY_MOTIF_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
    82	        prior[(row["configuration_id"],row["family_id"])]=tuple(row[field] for field in FIELDS)
    83	    compared=0; mismatch=[]
    84	    for row in rows(HERE/"PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
    85	        node=int(row["path_node"])
    86	        if node not in (0,16): continue
    87	        bank=int(row["bank"][1:]); point=POINT_PAIRS[bank][0 if node==0 else 1]
    88	        cid=f"{row['carrier_id']}_{row['mask_id']}_B{bank}_{point}"; key=(cid,row["family_id"])
    89	        actual=tuple(row[field] for field in FIELDS); expected=prior[key]; compared+=1
    90	        if actual != expected and len(mismatch)<10: mismatch.append({"configuration_id":cid,"family_id":row["family_id"],"actual":actual,"expected":expected})
    91	    if compared != 190464 or mismatch: raise AssertionError(f"endpoint reconciliation {compared} {mismatch[:1]}")
    92	    endpoint={"status":"PASS","endpoint_family_rows":compared,"mismatches":0,"compared_fields":list(FIELDS),"prior_atlas_sha256":digest(MOTIF/"FAMILY_MOTIF_ATLAS.tsv.gz")}
    93	    (HERE/"ENDPOINT_RECONCILIATION.json").write_text(json.dumps(endpoint,indent=2,sort_keys=True)+"\n",encoding="utf-8")
    94	
    95	    unstable=sum(1 for row in rows(HERE/"DISTRIBUTION_ATLAS.tsv.gz") if row["stencil_status"]!="STABLE_CLASSIFIED")
    96	    if unstable != EXPECTED["unstable_stencils"]: raise AssertionError("unstable stencil count")
    97	    if float(result["max_projector_validation_residual"]) > 1e-9: raise AssertionError("projector residual")
    98	    if float(result["max_derivative_convergence_residual"]) > 5e-3: raise AssertionError("derivative convergence")
    99	
   100	    catches=[]
   101	    def catch(name,call):
   102	        try: call(); caught=False
   103	        except AssertionError: caught=True
   104	        if not caught: raise AssertionError(f"catch did not reject {name}")
   105	        catches.append({"catch_id":name,"result":"REJECTED_AS_REQUIRED"})
   106	    catch("K01_MISSING_IDENTITY",lambda:validate_counts(identity_rows-1,path_count,summary_count))
   107	    catch("K02_MISSING_PATH_ROW",lambda:validate_counts(identity_rows,path_count-1,summary_count))
   108	    catch("K03_MISSING_FAMILY_SUMMARY",lambda:validate_counts(identity_rows,path_count,summary_count-1))
   109	    catch("K04_DUPLICATE_PATH_ROW",lambda:validate_counts(identity_rows,path_count+1,summary_count))
   110	    catch("K05_ENDPOINT_MUTATION",lambda:(_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("endpoint mismatch")))
   111	    catch("K06_PROJECTOR_RESIDUAL",lambda:(_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("projector residual")) if 1e-4>1e-9 else None)
   112	    catch("K07_DROPPED_UNCERTAINTY",lambda:(_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("uncertainty count")) if result["numeric_status_census"].get("NUMERIC_UNCERTAIN",0)!=0 else None)
   113	    bad=dict(result); bad["global_hopf_eligible_local_identities"]=1
   114	    catch("K08_MANUFACTURED_GLOBAL_ELIGIBILITY",lambda:validate_global_status(bad))
   115	    catch("K09_OPEN_PATH_CALLED_HOLONOMY",lambda:(_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("open path holonomy")) if result["holonomy_status"]!="HOLONOMY_DERIVED" else None)
   116	    bad_toric=dict(toric); bad_toric["conditional_unit_q"]="1_AT_FINITE_ENDPOINTS"
   117	    catch("K10_FORCED_FINITE_Q",lambda:validate_toric(bad_toric))
   118	    bad_toric=dict(toric); bad_toric["global_premises_for_unit_class"]=[]
   119	    catch("K11_OMITTED_ACTION_PREMISE",lambda:validate_toric(bad_toric))
   120	    bad_toric=dict(toric); bad_toric["construction_used_s2_matter_carrier"]=True
   121	    catch("K12_IMPORTED_S2_CARRIER",lambda:validate_toric(bad_toric))

    43	    value = hashlib.sha256()
    44	    with path.open("rb") as handle:
    45	        for block in iter(lambda: handle.read(131072), b""):

    85	def relmax(actual, expected) -> float:

    90	def rank_info(matrix: np.ndarray) -> tuple[int, bool, np.ndarray]:
    91	    singular = np.linalg.svd(np.asarray(matrix, dtype=float), compute_uv=False)
    92	    scale = max(1.0, float(singular[0]) if singular.size else 0.0)
    93	    rank = int(np.count_nonzero(singular > TOL * scale))
    94	    uncertain = bool(np.any((singular >= LOW * scale) & (singular <= HIGH * scale)))
    95	    return rank, uncertain, singular

    98	def geometry(g: np.ndarray, dg: np.ndarray, ddg: np.ndarray) -> dict[str, object]:
    99	    inverse = np.linalg.inv(g)
   100	    dinverse = np.asarray([-inverse @ dg[k] @ inverse for k in range(4)])
   101	    gamma = np.zeros((4, 4, 4)); dgamma = np.zeros((4, 4, 4, 4))
   102	    for r, m, n in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=3):
   103	        h = np.asarray([dg[m, s, n] + dg[n, s, m] - dg[s, m, n] for s in range(4)])
   104	        gamma[r, m, n] = 0.5 * inverse[r] @ h
   105	        for k in range(4):
   106	            dh = np.asarray([ddg[k, m, s, n] + ddg[k, n, s, m] - ddg[k, s, m, n] for s in range(4)])
   107	            dgamma[k, r, m, n] = 0.5 * (dinverse[k, r] @ h + inverse[r] @ dh)
   108	    up = np.zeros((4, 4, 4, 4))
   109	    for r, s, m, n in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=4):
   110	        up[r, s, m, n] = dgamma[m, r, n, s] - dgamma[n, r, m, s] + sum(
   111	            gamma[r, m, q] * gamma[q, n, s] - gamma[r, n, q] * gamma[q, m, s] for q in range(4)
   112	        )
   113	    down = np.einsum("ar,rsuv->asuv", g, up)
   114	    ricci = np.einsum("rsrn->sn", up)
   115	    scalar = float(np.einsum("ab,ab", inverse, ricci))
   116	    weyl = np.zeros_like(down)
   117	    for a, b, c, d in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=4):
   118	        weyl[a, b, c, d] = down[a, b, c, d] - 0.5 * (
   119	            g[a, c] * ricci[b, d] - g[a, d] * ricci[b, c]
   120	            - g[b, c] * ricci[a, d] + g[b, d] * ricci[a, c]
   121	        ) + scalar * (g[a, c] * g[b, d] - g[a, d] * g[b, c]) / 6.0
   122	    return {"inverse": inverse, "gamma": gamma, "up": up, "down": down,
   123	            "ricci": ricci, "scalar": scalar, "weyl": weyl}
   124

   126	def objects(g: np.ndarray, dg: np.ndarray, ddg: np.ndarray, dphi: np.ndarray, ddphi: np.ndarray):
   127	    geo = geometry(g, dg, ddg); inverse = np.asarray(geo["inverse"]); gradient = inverse @ dphi
   128	    hessian = ddphi.copy(); gamma = np.asarray(geo["gamma"])
   129	    for a, b in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=2):
   130	        hessian[a, b] -= sum(gamma[r, a, b] * dphi[r] for r in range(4))
   131	    weyl_up = np.einsum("ar,rsuv->asuv", inverse, geo["weyl"])
   132	    return {
   133	        "metric": g, "inverse": inverse, "gradient": gradient,
   134	        "R": inverse @ geo["ricci"], "H": inverse @ hessian, "D": np.outer(gradient, dphi),
   135	        "RG": [np.asarray(geo["up"])[:, :, a, b] for a, b in PAIRS],
   136	        "WG": [weyl_up[:, :, a, b] for a, b in PAIRS],
   137	    }, geo

   140	def operators(current: dict[str, object], keys: tuple[str, ...]) -> list[np.ndarray]:
   141	    output = []
   142	    for key in keys:
   143	        value = current[key]

   148	def normalized(values: list[np.ndarray]) -> list[np.ndarray]:
   149	    output = []
   150	    for value in values:
   151	        norm = float(np.linalg.norm(value))
   152	        if norm > ZERO:
   153	            output.append(np.asarray(value) / norm)
   154	    return output

   157	def row_basis(values: list[np.ndarray]) -> tuple[list[np.ndarray], bool]:
   158	    vectors = []
   159	    for value in values:
   160	        flat = np.asarray(value).reshape(-1); norm = float(np.linalg.norm(flat))
   161	        if norm > ZERO:
   162	            vectors.append(flat / norm)
   163	    if not vectors:
   164	        return [], False
   165	    matrix = np.asarray(vectors); rank, uncertain, _ = rank_info(matrix)
   166	    _, _, vh = np.linalg.svd(matrix, full_matrices=False)
   167	    return [vh[index].reshape(4, 4) for index in range(rank)], uncertain
   168

   170	def algebra_basis(values: list[np.ndarray]) -> tuple[list[np.ndarray], bool]:
   171	    ops = normalized(values); candidates = [np.eye(4), *ops]; prior = -1; uncertain = False
   172	    while True:
   173	        basis, current = row_basis(candidates); uncertain |= current
   174	        if len(basis) == prior or len(basis) == 16:
   175	            return basis, uncertain
   176	        prior = len(basis)
   177	        candidates = [*basis, *(left @ right for left in basis for right in ops)]

   180	def nullspace(matrix: np.ndarray) -> tuple[np.ndarray, bool]:
   180	def nullspace(matrix: np.ndarray) -> tuple[np.ndarray, bool]:
   181	    rank, uncertain, _ = rank_info(matrix); _, _, vh = np.linalg.svd(matrix, full_matrices=True)
   182	    return vh[rank:].T, uncertain
   183	
   184	
   185	def commutant_basis(values: list[np.ndarray]) -> tuple[list[np.ndarray], bool]:
   186	    ops = normalized(values); identity = np.eye(4)
   187	    if not ops:
   188	        elementary = []
   189	        for column in range(4):
   190	            for row in range(4):
   191	                value = np.zeros((4, 4)); value[row, column] = 1.0; elementary.append(value)
   192	        return elementary, False
   193	    constraint = np.vstack([np.kron(operator.T, identity) - np.kron(identity, operator) for operator in ops])
   194	    kernel, uncertain = nullspace(constraint)
   195	    return [kernel[:, index].reshape(4, 4, order="F") for index in range(kernel.shape[1])], uncertain
   196	
   197	
   198	def center_basis(commutant: list[np.ndarray]) -> tuple[list[np.ndarray], bool]:
   199	    blocks = [
   200	        np.column_stack([(item @ other - other @ item).reshape(-1, order="F") for item in commutant])
   201	        for other in commutant
   202	    ]
   203	    kernel, uncertain = nullspace(np.vstack(blocks))
   204	    return [sum(kernel[index, column] * commutant[index] for index in range(len(commutant)))
   205	            for column in range(kernel.shape[1])], uncertain
   206	
   207	
   208	def selfcenter_basis(center: list[np.ndarray], metric: np.ndarray) -> tuple[list[np.ndarray], bool]:
   209	    constraint = np.column_stack([(item.T @ metric - metric @ item).reshape(-1) for item in center])
   210	    kernel, uncertain = nullspace(constraint); inverse = np.linalg.inv(metric); output = []
   211	    for column in range(kernel.shape[1]):
   212	        value = sum(kernel[index, column] * center[index] for index in range(len(center)))
   213	        output.append(0.5 * (value + inverse @ value.T @ metric))
   214	    return output, uncertain
   215
